<!-- paragraph:1394 para_id:00000572 style:Normal -->
Cut content

Maya paused, her gaze sweeping over the chamber, and she felt the words she had rehearsed begin to slip away. The speech had been painstakingly crafted to emphasize the tradition and purpose of the High Clades, but something inside her rebelled. She tightened her grip on the edge of the dais and took a breath.

<!-- paragraph:1395 para_id:00000573 style:Normal -->
"But today, I am not here to simply repeat the traditions of our ancestors." Her voice rose slightly, cutting through the stillness. "Last night, our citadel was attacked."

<!-- paragraph:1396 para_id:00000574 style:Normal -->
A ripple of unease swept through the chamber, though no one spoke. Maya’s eyes darted to Velkor Nyctaris, who stiffened, his lips parting as if to interrupt. She raised her voice before he could speak.

<!-- paragraph:1397 para_id:00000575 style:Normal -->
"You all know about it," she pressed, her tone sharp, her gaze cutting through the chamber. "Your agents would have already reported back, wouldn’t they? Perhaps they told you that our walls held firm, that we stood unshaken against the strength arrayed against us. And perhaps they also mentioned that many of the attackers died—not by lightning, but by fire."

<!-- paragraph:1398 para_id:00000576 style:Normal -->
Her words carried a biting edge of sarcasm as she scanned the faces of the High Clade magi. She saw their discomfort, the unease creeping into their carefully controlled expressions.

<!-- paragraph:1399 para_id:00000577 style:Normal -->
"You know what that means." Her voice turned colder, her gaze cutting to each High Clade in turn. "It means I was there. It means I fought back. And it means that if the attack was meant to make me falter, to scare me, or to eliminate me entirely, it failed."

<!-- paragraph:1400 para_id:00000578 style:Normal -->
Velkor leaned forward, his voice low and firm. "Lady Maya—"

<!-- paragraph:1401 para_id:00000579 style:Normal -->
She overrode him, her words surging with fire. "I know the High Clades, as do we all. Perhaps the attack was meant to gain position, to strike at Rezin under the guise of chaos. Perhaps someone thought to exploit our moment of transition. But let me make this clear: I am done with the scheming and killing that has consumed our kind for no purpose other than self-interest."

<!-- paragraph:1402 para_id:0000057A style:Normal -->
She took a step forward, her Shroud shimmering faintly at the edges as she stood tall, her voice ringing out like a challenge. "The attackers suffered for their mistake. Many of them will never return. And when we find out who sent them, perhaps the rest of you will get to experience what it is like to stand with only five High Clades instead of six."

<!-- paragraph:1404 para_id:0000057C style:Normal -->
Her gaze swept the chamber, her pulse steadying as the weight of the moment sank in. Her eyes found Niall, seated in their family’s box, his posture regal yet relaxed. His smile was faint but unmistakable—a proud, rare expression that made her chest swell with emotion. Yet, there was something distant in his gaze, as though he was seeing beyond the chamber, to a memory or a future only he could perceive.

<!-- paragraph:1406 para_id:0000057E style:Normal -->
“What you did today,” he began, his voice low but weighted, “will be seen as a challenge.”

<!-- paragraph:1407 para_id:0000057F style:Normal -->
Maya blinked, her Shroud flickering faintly to life as her nerves responded to his tone. “A challenge?” she echoed, her mind racing to keep up.

<!-- paragraph:1408 para_id:00000580 style:Normal -->
“To the other High Clades,” he said. “Your words, your magic—it wasn’t just defiance, Maya. It was a statement. They’ll view it as a declaration of strength. And strength, among us, is always tested.”

<!-- paragraph:1409 para_id:00000581 style:Normal -->
Maya hesitated, unsure how to respond. “What does that mean?” she finally asked.

<!-- paragraph:1410 para_id:00000582 style:Normal -->
He exhaled slowly, the sound heavy with meaning. “It means you’re the one who issued the challenge—whether you intended to or not. So, you will be the one they target. While you’re within the citadel, the Registry will keep you safe. But once you step outside, you must always keep your Shroud up. Always.”

<!-- paragraph:1412 para_id:00000584 style:Normal -->
Maya’s chest tightened, anger and disbelief warring within her. “That’s not—” she started, but he cut her off.

<!-- paragraph:1413 para_id:00000585 style:Normal -->
“Your wild explosions of magic,” he said coldly, “could have killed our own troops. That’s what comes from letting emotions creep in. Fear, anger, grief—they’re distractions. And distractions are deadly.”

# Endgame matchups

<!-- paragraph:1418 para_id:0000058A style:Normal -->
Setting up the attack
They go to take out Archeon first
They have a trap for Niall, to send him below ground. Magi are slower to register energies that are non-aligned with their hereditary magic. At the same time, ones that are can be distracting - how to set traps 101

<!-- paragraph:1420 para_id:0000058C style:Normal -->
Davian and Maya fighting Serathis, Drosin, and numerous Archeon un-Presented magi

Is that more impactful than her talking to Maya about how she’d never understand? Or could they have that convo, and then Davian fights her instead, so Maya and Niall can go to get the Heart?

Who fights who at the end of the book?

General sequence - more training at the citadel, Maya and Davian get to hang out and learn stuff. Drakhals/Archeon show up to make a deal (but secretly to try to goad Niall into a death trap). Maya/Niall/Davian/Harvick then attack.

<!-- paragraph:1425 para_id:00000591 style:Normal -->
Serathis wants it all. How does that affect her plans and alliances?

<!-- paragraph:1426 para_id:00000592 style:Normal -->
Matchups:
- Ultimate end state (work backwards): Maya and Niall vs Vorren, Davian joins
- Niall wants to fight Vorren alone, Maya is like “don’t be stupid”. Vorren is pleased.
- Davian is off rescuing his mother from Archeon. What if he just fights Drosin and Serathis is off to fight Maya?
- Serathis / Drosin

<!-- paragraph:1427 para_id:00000593 style:Normal -->
What if they walk into Archeon together?
- There is a trap of some kind to isolate Niall, by having him fall deep underground while Maya and Davian are attacked by Serathis and Drosin. Since Maya already fought Serathis and Drosin to a standstill, Serathis likely will bring in a bunch of other Archeon magi to help her out. This also provides some opportunities for Davian to “save” Maya.
- Maya and Davian are fighting Archeon together but Drosin and a bunch of unPresented are more focused on Maya, and Serathis is focused on Davian (or vice versa). That gives the opportunity for Serathis to stab Davian with the anti-Archeon knives (and for him to not die because the Ink Boon won’t let him while Maya isn’t nearby).
- Harvick is able to at least not die while fighting un-Presented Archeon
- Niall POV? He fights Vorren by himself and is really on the ropes.
- Maya finished off Serathis, letting Davian take the anti-Archeon knives. Maya leaves to help Niall while Davian kills the rest of Archeon (or they just run away) and frees his mother.
- This can have a scene where Davian chooses to go help Maya and Niall instead of just staying with his mother, or something. Harvick can take Kelyra out.
- Then, Davian joins Maya and Niall and all three of them together kill Vorren (barely). Elric surprise attacks and kills Davian while they’re all barely standing, Maya ruptures fate to save Davian, and then Elric regains some of his consciousness and runs away with an Ink Boon.

<!-- paragraph:1428 para_id:00000594 style:Normal -->
Serathis fighting Maya and Davian
- I beat you and Drosin before. -yes but you came to my home… and I have so many children. (She doesn’t care how many of them die)

<!-- paragraph:1429 para_id:00000595 style:Normal -->
Who are the friendly players?
- Maya. Very powerful and increasingly able to hold her own in hand to hand combat.
- Niall. Historically powerful but crippled by depression and especially vulnerable underground (which he may not understand deeply).
- Davian. Strong at basic hand to hand. At this point his Shroud should be fairly stable. He should have a mild to moderate understanding of “ki manipulation” and a similar grip on his Archeon hereditary magic. He also has Antithesis. Maya, Niall, and Davian all have speed of thought which they should be able to use fairly well at this point. To list:
	- Martial arts
	- Shroud arts
	- “ki manipulation”
	- Hereditary magic
	- A knife
	- Think fast
Note that the Archeon training is designed to blend the first three things together, allowing most of the cognitive capacity to be dedicated to using hereditary magic.
- Harvick: not able to shroud but has strong swordsmanship, a special sword, and “ki manipulation” that is not augmented by a Shroud.

<!-- paragraph:1431 para_id:00000597 style:Normal -->
Who are the enemy players?
- Serathis. She essentially is high clade level and her grand-children and great-grandchildren etc are a disgrace to her. She may have special anti-Archeon knives that she has as insurance against someone trying to unseat her, and can fight with them like she did “on the streets” like Kelyra.

<!-- paragraph:1432 para_id:00000598 style:Normal -->
What if Serathis knives are insurance against any rogue Archeon that want to challenge her? And they are specifically designed to counter them- stabs Davian but the ink heals him because Maya isn’t there? “You think you get to my age atop a pile of disgraceful backstabbing children, staying Head Magus, without a backup plan?”

<!-- paragraph:1434 para_id:0000059A style:Normal -->
Drosin (he’s the one still alive?). He is essentially High Clade level as long as he uses his gauntlets. To review, the Archeon technique is Shroud strength amplification multiplied by “ki manipulation” combined with energy storage and manipulation that are enabled by speed of thought. That sounds complicated but it boils down to: special punch, Shroud make stronger, move energy around by thinking fast.

<!-- paragraph:1436 para_id:0000059C style:Normal -->
Vorren. He is at this point likely the most powerful Drakhal, although if he had to fight Evana and Caius together he would have a hard time (although he’s certainly considered it). Caius gleefully “banished” Vorren to ensure his spot as the heir, but Vorren doesn’t care at all, the only thing he cares about is killing Niall, Maya, or anyone else powerful - he finds this deeply satisfying and is gleeful at the thought of this himself to the point he barely noticed the banishment. Of course, Evana is smart enough that she keeps Vorren around as a tool, knowing that having a disavowable ultra powerful murder weapon is very useful.
- Vorren is also a perfect deterrent to any Ink Boon users that start to think they could overthrow the Harbingers. He may kill some of them just for fun.
- Now that Vorren has the Heart, he is able to power his techniques with unlimited energy. Unlike Maya being bound by the heat available near her (remembering the distance law for magical effort) he has unlimited force that he can draw out from an object he holds. His power is still limited by his ability to channel and use that force, however.

<!-- paragraph:1437 para_id:0000059D style:Normal -->
Random cool note: if Drakhal drains kinetic energy from everything around them, then right before they attack everything might go utterly dead silent (how is that different from heat, if heat is just undirected kinetic energy?)

<!-- paragraph:1439 para_id:0000059F style:Normal -->
Caius - unlikely to be involved as he can be a major antagonist later.

<!-- paragraph:1441 para_id:000005A1 style:Normal -->
Evana - also highly unlikely to be involved from a political perspective

<!-- paragraph:1443 para_id:000005A3 style:Normal -->
Elric - only joining in at the end to kill Davian with a surprise attack, regaining much of his cognitive abilities after Maya fractures fate, and also having the benefits of Ink Boons

<!-- paragraph:1445 para_id:000005A5 style:Title -->
# Other endgame fight notes

<!-- paragraph:1446 para_id:000005A6 style:Normal -->
End of book fights
Think about end matchups. Serathis with knives vs Maya? Saying she learned them when she was young on the streets or w/e? Davian vs brann? Evana, Caius, etc?

<!-- paragraph:1447 para_id:000005A7 style:Normal -->
Attacking Archeon
Niall having Maya blow up the watch towers at range. Then coming into Archeon and just indiscriminately killing everyone because “they could all be magi, we can’t let them get close”. They’re all randos put there by Serathis for him to kill while she holds all her magi in reserve.

<!-- paragraph:1448 para_id:000005A8 style:Normal -->
Niall is ambushed
Niall attacking Serathis - he yells about her thinking he’s weak and underestimating him. Raises his arms up and every window in the hall explodes inwards with lightning, wildly forking in all directions around the room. He takes a step forward - that’s when Maya (or Davian) notices the distraction / trap - and the floor explodes / collapses under Niall (with Davian pulling Maya back).

<!-- paragraph:1449 para_id:000005A9 style:Normal -->
The hall that Niall confronts Serathis in is kind of like a cathedral, with painted glass windows that he shatters. “They used to worship the Creator here. Ridiculous. What use does a Creator of all things have for worship? He wound up the clock and placed it on the mantle.” “All we use the Creator’s name for today is as a curse.”

<!-- paragraph:1450 para_id:000005AA style:Normal -->
The people Niall kills at Archeon when he blows all the windows in are just random un-powered children and servants. After Niall kills them he approaches Serathis right as Maya and Davian realize something is wrong, and Serathis says the above and triggers her trap.

<!-- paragraph:1451 para_id:000005AB style:Normal -->
When Niall kills everyone Maya notices the lack of a shroud flash

<!-- paragraph:1452 para_id:000005AC style:Normal -->
Niall storms into Archeon yelling about “how weak do you think I am?” And how they misjudged him etc. when they get to the main hall Serathis is there and Niall storms ahead, some lightning and flame traps go off and he brushes them aside. Davian wonders about this and he pulls Maya back right before a big kinetic trap goes off - remembering that power-aligned energy can be distracting to a magus.

<!-- paragraph:1453 para_id:000005AD style:Normal -->
“Did you think we didn’t understand that the issue wasn’t your strength, but your ability to change? To see the new paths?”

<!-- paragraph:1454 para_id:000005AE style:Normal -->
Niall fights Vorren by himself

<!-- paragraph:1455 para_id:000005AF style:Normal -->
Vorren wants to kill Niall, and with the Heart take his place as the undisputed controller of the world. He thinks that with Niall dead and his own power boosted, he can by himself rule over all of the cities and conquer the surrounding areas, a limitless ambition that he’s waited many years to fulfill.

<!-- paragraph:1456 para_id:000005B0 style:Normal -->
Maya fights Serathis
The high clades want you to think progress comes from hoarding, from accumulation, from refinement. But progress is truly unpredictable, it comes in leaps and bounds from those who are willing to claw their way up from the bottom.

<!-- paragraph:1457 para_id:000005B1 style:Normal -->
Davian fights Drosin; Kelyra manifests a Shroud
Davia is fighting Drosin and knows Kelyra has a mental block against manifesting a Shroud, to protect herself (Drosin may mention this). He asks Kelyra to help him / protect him instead of only wanting revenge and hating Archeon. He throws his knife at Drosin, who dodges, and Kelyra manifests her Shroud to break free, grab the knife, and stab Drosin in the back.

<!-- paragraph:1458 para_id:000005B2 style:Normal -->
Davian to Kelyra - you’ve just been such a slave to your fear of Archeon and your hate of the high clades, and I don’t want to be a slave to it too.

<!-- paragraph:1459 para_id:000005B3 style:Normal -->
Davian is fighting Drosin to free Kelyra, she can’t shroud. He tells her about the slave thing and then asks for her help, he throws the knife at Drosin who dodges it. Then Kelyra manifests a shroud, grabs the knife, and stabs Drosin in the back. They go to fight Serathis - Maya has been fighting / talking with her for a while, Serathis just throws grandchildren at her to slow her down since she expects Vorren to kill Niall and then come kill Maya. Davian and Kelyra come to fight Serathis to free Maya up, ?Davian tells Kelyra he likes Maya or something which makes her less hesitant? When they kill Serathis, Kelyra takes the dual knives and challenges the rest of Archeon to test her, and tells Davian if it’s important to him he should go to Maya. He protests but she says let me help you and he agrees.

Serathis makes it clear that it’s a disappointment because she has the speed of thought and martial arts skills but never manifested. -endgame, Maya fights Serathis and the other archeon while davian fights drosin to free Kelyra. Serathis has dual knives with returning bracers like Harvick. -Kelyra manifests her shroud and kills Drosin, this can be related to Davian finally letting her help him (vs in prologue where she asks to help him and he says no). Then Davian and Kelyra fight Serathis while Maya goes to assist Niall. Kelyra kills Serathis by catching the returning knives and stabbing her. Serathis is thrilled to finally be able to die happy knowing she has an heir that is just like she envisioned. She puts a bloody hand on Kelyra’s face and says, wasn’t it all worth it daughter? Kelyra says no. Serathis asks Kelyra to burn down all the high clades. -kelyra is injured during the fight so Davian goes by himself to help Maya and Niall, maybe Kelyra is mollified about the high clades because Maya helped Davian (but also says it could be self interest).

<!-- paragraph:1488 para_id:000005D0 style:Normal -->
When they’re underground Maya fights Archeon on her own to save Niall’s strength. They’re too predictable for her now that she knows their trick

<!-- paragraph:1489 para_id:000005D1 style:Normal -->
“If you’re narrow-minded, you are specialized and focused, undistracted (is something an evil person would say)”

<!-- paragraph:1490 para_id:000005D2 style:Normal -->
From Serathis’ perspective, anything Maya accomplishes is just because of her genetic heritage and privileged upbringing. That makes her bitter to lose despite feeling like she clawed her way up from the bottom.

<!-- paragraph:1491 para_id:000005D3 style:Normal -->
The Archeon high magus is angry at how Maya can “effortlessly” just be born into powerful magic, when her family had to claw her way up from the bottom of the Low Clades through research, techniques, breeding, etc. They’ve been doing their breeding program since before she was born, and she was the first ‘successful’ one born to the prior Low Clade. Then they killed off the High Clade that was in the citadel they’re in now. She frames it as clawing up from the slums in that city, because maybe it’s an especially bad mini city-state

<!-- paragraph:1492 para_id:000005D4 style:Normal -->
The Archeon head magus could get an ink boon and fight Maya by herself. Maya can be thinking, it’s a new tool for her - she was too proud to use one before. She’ll have the same predictability and limitations, just be faster. She may also have throwing knives (think Madame Butterfly) or other tools, being like I am giving up my pride to kill you or something.

<!-- paragraph:1493 para_id:000005D5 style:Normal -->
Davian and his mother were probably both using Subversion incorrectly and inefficiently. His mom made up the name Subversion based on her own ideas about it. She just saw the ability to dissipate other magics, or release their energy, and thought that’s all there is to it. But it actually allows transformation of any energy. Normally shrouds are used to convert any kind of energy to one aligned with your hereditary magic. Archeon magic can convert or alter or store any kind of energy but they lack the generation abilities of hereditary magic. So they’re stuck trying to amplify martial techniques with their shrouds, use tools, etc. doing all that at once makes them predictable. Serathis wanted someone with a faster and broader ability to use Subversion, which would require a lot more technical mental prowess (like how Niall and Maya’s speed of thought amplifies their magic). Serathis unfortunately never produced someone as strong as her, before Kelyra. Subconsciously her rejection of using tools herself reflects her desire to be a full High Clade magus in truth, without deception. Instead she has to rely on group attacks, sneak attacks, deception about abilities, etc. her children all learn from her that this is the way to succeed.

None of the Archeon magi could have done what Davian did with the sphere. The ink by controlling him gave him a higher level of power because he wasn’t thinking other thoughts or conflicted.

<!-- paragraph:1663 para_id:0000067F style:Normal -->
Okay honing in on the whole jinwright thing - jin are magical circuit components - to some extent they’re derived by the understanding that hereditary magic also runs on “circuits” somehow (or does it lol). Each ji is etched with a different metal and pattern based on its function (capacitor, resistor, etc). Note that like when I was in high school, Cole and I were able to build that rail cannon based off schematics. It might seem like it would be super hard but it’s more just following instructions and double checking. the real work is knowing enough that you can idiot check yourself in terms of placements, power throughput, etc.

<!-- paragraph:1664 para_id:00000680 style:Normal -->
⁃	there are "power” jin that act like batteries, where the material they are etched into slowly degrades, powering the glyph lattice

<!-- paragraph:1665 para_id:00000681 style:Normal -->
⁃	Old ji tech - like in the citadel - uses big ji. There are ways to miniaturize but they’re very expensive and not practical for normal use. (Which is why few people can do it, and Niall has to go through one of them - and Archeon finds out due to using the same people)

# Overarching changes

<!-- paragraph:2054 para_id:00000806 style:Normal -->

<!-- paragraph:2057 para_id:00000809 style:Normal -->
“All stories have been told before. We tell them to ourselves, as did all men who ever were. And all men who will ever be. The only things new are the names.”

<!-- paragraph:2059 para_id:0000080B style:Normal -->
remember you can ask Chat if you’re stuck!

<!-- paragraph:2060 para_id:0000080C style:Normal -->
Just get the skeleton down, you can always improve the writing or edit scenes later

<!-- paragraph:2062 para_id:0000080E style:Normal -->
General points

<!-- paragraph:2063 para_id:0000080F style:Normal -->
Emphasize that the clothing they all wear is specifically designed to make them look good and elegant and wealthy and secure while killing tons of people

<!-- paragraph:2064 para_id:00000810 style:Normal -->
Spells should be really taxing mentally and require a lot of thinking, which is why mental improvement makes them better. All of the unrealistic abilities are amplifications of normal things by the distortion in reality that makes it more responsive to thought

<!-- paragraph:2065 para_id:00000811 style:Normal -->
Power usage - visualization of strands linking things together. Holding open channels to push energy down. Having to hold many in the mind at once - something the magi are bred to be able to do (but if unregulated, then it just all goes off in random directions with more backlash)

<!-- paragraph:2066 para_id:00000812 style:Normal -->
Fighting should always be very experiential, focusing on how hands feel, feet moving, etc - if possible

<!-- paragraph:2067 para_id:00000813 style:Normal -->
Next draft - give everyone names, Maya should know her guards’ names, Davian should be talking to Concord members. -slower romance -more magical tech /zan. Look for things that are boring and either spice them up or abstract them

<!-- paragraph:2068 para_id:00000814 style:Normal -->
In the rewrite, it’s okay to drag the romance wayyyyyyy out and have them kissing be kind of impulsive and random, and still be conflicted and testy thru the end of the book.

<!-- paragraph:2069 para_id:00000815 style:Normal -->
De-emphasize speed of thought? It makes for some awkward scenes. Emphasizing schema more would be thematic. We can still talk about reaction time etc, but just show people thinking fast instead of really emphasizing slow motion.

<!-- paragraph:2070 para_id:00000816 style:Normal -->
What if people from Naeroth are like a different species and Maya is half bred? Purple? - her mom speaks in poorly translated idioms “I’m not going to hold onto your time” (instead of “keep you” etc)

<!-- paragraph:2071 para_id:00000817 style:Normal -->
Preface/epilogue
We are all unreliable narrators. What does the way I wrote the book say about me, and what does the way you read it say about you?

<!-- paragraph:2072 para_id:00000818 style:Normal -->
During rewrites need to focus a lot more on speed of thought and how that impacts things. And if everyone’s is slightly different… like Maya’s 3D visualization is crazy, she can map out a lot more spatial things in her mind (Niall is like that too - important for their kinds of magic).

<!-- paragraph:2073 para_id:00000819 style:Normal -->
Melissa likes how Kaladin keeps getting beaten way down but then becomes OP. Think about that when rewriting scenes. That can happen to Maya, Davian, and Niall each in different scenes

<!-- paragraph:2074 para_id:0000081A style:Normal -->
How does a magus’ enhanced brain see things differently? You did it well with Kelyra. Pile on the worldbuilding elements to make it interesting. The money, the zän, the powers, the political elements, the nomenclature, the language… the more it’s hooked in the better. Of course I can always rewrite to increase it.

<!-- paragraph:2075 para_id:0000081B style:Normal -->
Chat probably breaks long quotes up more than it needs to. It’s okay for them to be long if they’re important.

<!-- paragraph:2076 para_id:0000081C style:Normal -->
Maya’s mother is some kind of demi-human from Naeroth. Maya has violet eyes. People are racist against them.

Prior scene edits
General scene notes (when rewriting)

<!-- paragraph:2078 para_id:0000081E style:Normal -->
All: experiential, and focusing on cognitive burden of what they’re doing

<!-- paragraph:2079 para_id:0000081F style:Normal -->
Davian: self-attributing bad motives (I’m just doing this to get them to trust me etc)

<!-- paragraph:2080 para_id:00000820 style:Normal -->
Maya: perfectionism, worrying that she needs to always be doing more, imposter syndrome

<!-- paragraph:2081 para_id:00000821 style:Normal -->
Davian and Maya to each other - unconditional positive regard. Where Niall might want to protect due to fear, Davian will support due to trust.

<!-- paragraph:2082 para_id:00000822 style:Normal -->
Magic: emphasize the cognitive load - it’s like taking a board exam, and your mind is just completely drained. The complex things go first. Magi are genetically trained to think quickly. Drawing channels (for energy flow) with the mind and holding them is a cognitive burden. The cognition for the shrouds “feels” different

<!-- paragraph:2083 para_id:00000823 style:Normal -->
Emphasizing these cognitive loads is going to be a big part of editing.

<!-- paragraph:2084 para_id:00000824 style:Normal -->
I like the idea that Niall’s hair is white, as some kind of side effect of his powers (Elric had it too).

<!-- paragraph:2085 para_id:00000825 style:Normal -->
Sub-luminescent use of magic won’t cause the sigil to glow - that’s the level Davian is using his subversion at to mitigate the effects of the ink boon

Re-design clothing - the concepts are good. Niall in military coat (he just says he’s attached to it from the time of the war and Maya assumes it has something to do with her mother). Maya in the sleeveless sort of elegant combat outfit

<!-- paragraph:2096 para_id:00000830 style:Normal -->

<!-- paragraph:2097 para_id:00000831 style:Normal -->
Integrate zän into more things. What powers them? Do they automate doors? Imagine red stone circuits in Minecraft. The power of the Rezin citadel was that the heart supplied limitless energy although the circuits still had to be re-etched they burned out passively rather than actively, lasting much longer.

Major edits

<!-- paragraph:2099 para_id:00000833 style:Normal -->
Big change - swapping Jalen for Kelyra

<!-- paragraph:2100 para_id:00000834 style:Normal -->
Kelyra was an Archeon running away from a birth contract with her daughter, after she met Jalen. She never was able to manifest a Shroud when young. After she had Selina, she started manifesting Subversion and ran away because Selina legally belonged to Archeon. She would have kept this secret and Davian was born after she left.

<!-- paragraph:2101 para_id:00000835 style:Normal -->
-Another swap - Alden is now named Aldira and is a woman

<!-- paragraph:2102 para_id:00000836 style:Normal -->
-Glyphs are renamed to jin (singular: ji), and a glyphwright is now a jinwright

<!-- paragraph:2103 para_id:00000837 style:Normal -->
-Magic is associated with accelerated thought. Shrouds and hereditary magic are distinct lineages

<!-- paragraph:2104 para_id:00000838 style:Normal -->

-Consider gluing short early chapters together if it works for continuity

<!-- paragraph:2106 para_id:0000083A style:Normal -->
-Antithesis is now a dagger - it has been a dagger the whole time rather than a sword. It’s a prototype for the Archeon gauntlets that Kelyra stole and made up a name and that it has been passed down in their family for generations.

<!-- paragraph:2107 para_id:0000083B style:Normal -->
- Call the threads of fate the Skein

<!-- paragraph:2108 para_id:0000083C style:Normal -->
- Central spire is gone. Each High Clade now runs a mini city-state but primarily focuses on their citadel (each area has different characteristics). Arena is in the middle.

<!-- paragraph:2109 para_id:0000083D style:Normal -->
- Change Evand Drakhal to Evana. It makes more sense that most high magi would be women, since position is determined by magical power and the women are the one having the children - so a powerful woman would both be the de facto head and the most likely to have lots of children.

<!-- paragraph:2110 para_id:0000083E style:Normal -->
- “Channeling” is carving / carved pathways. “He carved out pathways for the charge, and it greedily flowed through them”. Make reference to “inverted space” or “inverted path” when talking about inversions of the natural law. “Rending” could be a more violent/less controlled version
- Sign language is phonetic and based on the same system as the zan script used by the Masked Clades
- Combat: fights should be more close range and visceral in general. This is the change that is coming because of Archeon’s innovation. Also emphasize the current long-range magic that is slower but the standard type of carving used by the High Clades because they’re still somewhat influenced by the “magus vs army” archetype. What warfare really is now is magus vs magus, with the army a distraction at best and a way to occupy territory / convey information.
- Treasury sphere = vault sphere

# Title stuff

<!-- paragraph:2151 para_id:00000867 style:Normal -->
Title

<!-- paragraph:2152 para_id:00000868 style:Normal -->
Ink and Brine? It’s not quite as punchy as Void and Brine but ties in better with the world. I could just emphasize the inkiness or something.

<!-- paragraph:2153 para_id:00000869 style:Normal -->
“A Shroud of Ink and Fury” (too similar to another popular book but it sounds cool)

<!-- paragraph:2154 para_id:0000086A style:Normal -->
(A) Shroud of Ink and Brine

<!-- paragraph:2155 para_id:0000086B style:Normal -->
dark threads of ink, bright threads/channels of fury (or flame) - interlocked motif overlying a man and woman. The girl of threads and flame. -threads is good - not too generic. Ink is good although more overused than you’d think. Brine is unique.

<!-- paragraph:2156 para_id:0000086C style:Normal -->
Dark Threads of Ink, Bright Threads of Flame (here the dark threads represent depression and trauma, and the bright threads represent anxiety and perfectionism)

<!-- paragraph:2157 para_id:0000086D style:Normal -->
All the World a Savage Garden” would have been a better title for that one book. But it’s from Anne Rice.

<!-- paragraph:2158 para_id:0000086E style:Normal -->
Translator’s note - not all translated words have 1:1 correlations within the English language. In most cases where multiple words could have been used, the most common English word was chosen. For ease of reading, in some cases multi-syllable common words have been replaced with slightly less common but shorter words. The base-six number system has been mostly converted into base ten, but be aware of the mental and cultural significance of even multiples of six. Words that are not native to the point of view character (mostly loan words) have been glossed phonetically.

<!-- paragraph:2172 para_id:0000087C style:Normal -->
more satisfying end. So reversing everything is kind of anti-acceptance. I think it’s reasonable that they use Selwin’s abilities to kill the deity. But, a lot of what has happened isn’t because of the softening of reality - it’s the choices people made, to be evil or not. So just removing him doesn’t remove everything that happened or guarantee the world will be perfect going forward. It’s accepting that prior trauma from a cosmic perspective, and believing that going forward we have the choice to try to make things better

<!-- paragraph:2264 para_id:000008D8 style:Normal -->
Subversion is about changing the form and shape/direction of energy. The inefficiencies of the transformation are reflected as a backlash to the user, so a more efficient transformation will result in less backlash and more power.

<!-- paragraph:2265 para_id:000008D9 style:Normal -->
Paradox is heavy and broad - fighting someone in a shroud is more like fighting someone in heavy armor, where you’d want a mace. There aren’t any weak points to try to slip an edge through so weight and momentum are better than sharpness

<!-- paragraph:2266 para_id:000008DA style:Normal -->
⁃	it also gives more mass and surface area for subversion to burn off backlash. There could be heat exchange fins or channels or something. It’s an item whose creation and sturdiness is fueled by magic

⁃	Maya / Niall (or Keylra?) design it

Some of the current low clades may be working on their own… but everyone’s combo is going to be different to get what they need to reach high clade status

<!-- paragraph:2370 para_id:00000942 style:Normal -->
Therapeutic interventions and “Void” versus healthy acceptance / “Brine”

<!-- paragraph:2371 para_id:00000943 style:Normal -->
“My brain still craves dissociation”

<!-- paragraph:2372 para_id:00000944 style:Normal -->
Taking the focus off yourself - how can I help others etc - reduces rumination and anxiety about how you present

<!-- paragraph:2373 para_id:00000945 style:Normal -->
Harvick is probably going to be the main “mule” for this. He already did mindfulness with Davian

<!-- paragraph:2374 para_id:00000946 style:Normal -->
A bubble within the brine - you’re acknowledging it’s there but not letting it throw you around. Or a ship?

<!-- paragraph:2375 para_id:00000947 style:Normal -->
Harvick could admit maybe he pushed Davian too far early on, and can suggest this technique instead of just falling into the Brine

<!-- paragraph:2376 para_id:00000948 style:Normal -->
“Really paying attention to what you’re thinking is not for the faint of heart… but that’s the only way to change it.”

<!-- paragraph:2377 para_id:00000949 style:Normal -->
Void vs Brine. “Void” represents no values and no thoughts/feelings, which allows magic to a certain point but would never reach the highest level. “Brine” represents being carried along by the present, accepting the bitterness of your past, and looking forward to the future.

<!-- paragraph:2378 para_id:0000094A style:Normal -->
Void is like “emotions just hold you back and distract you” which is really just kinda edgy, and also completely removing emotions isn’t possible or probably desirable

<!-- paragraph:2379 para_id:0000094B style:Normal -->
Values are the only thing that can cause you pain. If you don’t value anything then you can’t be hurt. At the same time, it removes the drive that makes us alive and human. Niall has been using “void” and Davian starts drifting into it, thinking he is “improving” on mindfulness but what he really needs is to accept what’s going on and work on how to make the future better.

<!-- paragraph:2380 para_id:0000094C style:Normal -->
When you’re dead do you want people to cry at your funeral? Well, that would be sad. Wouldn’t it be sadder if no one cried?

<!-- paragraph:2381 para_id:0000094D style:Normal -->
Niall’s magic is weaker because he hasn’t accepted and worked on his values, and he’s depressed. Subversion is also a high-clade-level magic, but the chronic depression and denial etc have prevented him from using it.

<!-- paragraph:2382 para_id:0000094E style:Normal -->
Acceptance doesn’t mean that the future can’t be different, it means you accept the present as it is to work towards the future

<!-- paragraph:2383 para_id:0000094F style:Normal -->
Davian is trying to “force it” with the void, as opposed to splitting / directing it with Brine (magic) which allows reduced backlash

<!-- paragraph:2384 para_id:00000950 style:Normal -->

⁃	to matter, Maya, for her to look at him like he does mean something

<!-- paragraph:2433 para_id:00000981 style:Normal -->
That is your motivation - and not thinking about it won’t change that

<!-- paragraph:2434 para_id:00000982 style:Normal -->

Depression reduces abstract reasoning so can impact casting if severe

That is her angle at acceptance - accepting what is, what can be, what is possible, rather than being blinded by pushing towards unrealistic ideals she got from an ill/overbearing father.

<!-- paragraph:2443 para_id:0000098B style:Normal -->

<!-- paragraph:2445 para_id:0000098D style:Normal -->
So the progression of magic development - it should feel like going through med school and residency. It’s super complicated and seems impossible, but eventually it becomes natural and you’re doing it easily. That’s modified by who you are and how smart (or naturally talented) you are as well

# Lore

<!-- paragraph:2456 para_id:00000998 style:Title -->
# Numbering system

<!-- paragraph:2457 para_id:00000999 style:Normal -->
Base 6 numbering system

<!-- paragraph:2459 para_id:0000099B style:Normal -->
Having 6 be the number instead of 7 represents the “off by one” issue of their reality. See notes for drawn version of 1-6. (The Rezins live in city 1 in between the second most powerful Drakhal and the least powerful Archeon)

<!-- paragraph:2460 para_id:0000099C style:Normal -->
Six day “weeks”. 一day, 二day etc. Hexday. Use the zan (crown-day etc but make it better). Six hexdays is a “month” and they do have a moon. Since a month is 6*6 days then it’s essentially “100” in base six. Are a month and 100 (36) the same term? “That’ll cost you a moon(sworth).” Base six - so 17 would be “two six n’ five”. 45 would be a moon, six n’ three.

<!-- paragraph:2461 para_id:0000099D style:Normal -->
Rough draft (think about things being etched/carved and how that would influence the cuts)

<!-- paragraph:2463 para_id:0000099F style:Title -->
# Worldbuilding depth

<!-- paragraph:2464 para_id:000009A0 style:Normal -->
Forerunners

<!-- paragraph:2465 para_id:000009A1 style:Normal -->
Older scouts who take hazardous positions working with magi in exchange for the promise of a large payout to their families if they die. That’s essentially Harvick’s position with Niall, and previously with Elric.

<!-- paragraph:2467 para_id:000009A3 style:Normal -->
Zan
- What zan do people have in day to day life? Making doors lighter, etc. Lighting rooms.

<!-- paragraph:2468 para_id:000009A4 style:Normal -->
- How are they used in communication and ciphers?
- What powers them? What do you do when they break down?

Sign language
- Who uses sign language? How do they use it?
- It is phonetic and zan-based, in some ciphers

<!-- paragraph:2470 para_id:000009A6 style:Normal -->
Magi minds
- How does having a magi mind affect the way you see things?
- Magi think very quickly
- Worldbuilding - how does Maya’s brain sense the world differently, attuned to heat and cold? How does being super rich affect what she has access to?

<!-- paragraph:2472 para_id:000009A8 style:Normal -->
Sigils
- Sigils are visual elements that show you have a power

<!-- paragraph:2473 para_id:000009A9 style:Normal -->
- How does this change the way Maya views herself? How about Davian?

Masks
- The Masked Clades wear masks. Davian carves a zan into his
- How does this line up with the metaphorical masks of the Clade system?

<!-- paragraph:2475 para_id:000009AB style:Normal -->
Cities and politics
- Each High Clade governs a legally distinct city. Zones within the city are governed by the Low Clades who divide responsibility up among them, depending on the city. The Rezins have a more central administrative organization, but generally all the city-wedges are treated as secondary to concerns inside of each citadel.

<!-- paragraph:2476 para_id:000009AC style:Normal -->
Citadels
- The Rezin’s Registry providing power and security is a huge advantage and encourages centralization

<!-- paragraph:2477 para_id:000009AD style:Normal -->
- Other High Clade citadels might have expanded their walls, built multiple sets of walls around their citadels, removed walls all together (outer walls - in favor of more secure inner walls).

<!-- paragraph:2479 para_id:000009AF style:Normal -->
Life spans
- How does having leaders that are both self-sufficient armies and able to live longer than everyone else affect politics and the perception of people beneath them?

<!-- paragraph:2481 para_id:000009B1 style:Normal -->
War
- Niall stopped war unilaterally and acts as a one-man nuclear deterrent
- Prior to Elric, Magi were not as universally powerful with stacked genetic abilities and acted in a valuable support role instead of in the front line
- With Archeon looking to upset the balance and allow magi to be targeted by close-range fighters (that may not even be Presented), war may revert to a slightly more traditional frame, with more support for High Clade magi
- Mercenary companies rely on high mobility rather than armor, and primarily use long-range arrows etc, sending volleys until the magus arrives and then retreating to safety to try to reduce casualties
- Large standing armies are not a part of the equation, citadel guards supported by and supporting magi instead

<!-- paragraph:2483 para_id:000009B3 style:Normal -->
Naeroth
- More traditional, complex zan that can power things more efficiently and longer but are much more expensive and less scalable
- More knowledge of fateweaving
- Isolationist

<!-- paragraph:2484 para_id:000009B4 style:Title -->
# City

<!-- paragraph:2485 para_id:000009B5 style:Normal -->
In each city-wedge they’re governed by their high Clade and are legally distinct cities

<!-- paragraph:2486 para_id:000009B6 style:Title -->
# Sign language

<!-- paragraph:2487 para_id:000009B7 style:Normal -->
『sign language』「sign language」

<!-- paragraph:2488 para_id:000009B8 style:Normal -->
In Chinese sign language, words are represented by phonetic components often, so the sign language used by the Masked Clades could be similar to their zän script - encoding the phonetic versions of words into signs. Theoretically each organization uses the same hand shapes but have different phonemes mapped to each one, so it would be very hard to parse someone else’s. In actual practice there’s probably a lot of overlap due to movement/communication between organizations, etc. No one wants to learn 20 different sign languages -short common articles etc have distinct hand shapes ex: 「you want [to be] seen. This [is not a] good idea.」

<!-- paragraph:2489 para_id:000009B9 style:Normal -->
Long words are likely abbreviated (what are some short one-syllable words that could be slang for longer words? “Ups” for High Clades or something? Maybe something cooler than that. I guess just “Highs”.

<!-- paragraph:2490 para_id:000009BA style:Title -->
# Magic notes

<!-- paragraph:2491 para_id:000009BB style:Normal -->
Magic simplification
- The current magic system is kind of unwieldy and cobbled together, which doesn’t make for good storytelling
- General fixes: Shrouds are now a reflex and only channeling lots of energy through them is cognitively exhausting.
	- Schema simplify descriptions of more complex magical activities. This removes having to describe in great detail how the different surfaces etc are used
	- Remove in-depth description of cognitive speed because it’s clunky and can be abstracted a bit anyway by just describing how quickly the character is thinking
	- Ink Pacts and reality warping magic all converge on the manipulation of the Skein, either by moving through a wrinkle in time, forcing a body into a prior state, or something like that.
	- Perceptions / cognition - might need to remove this element because it’s just another thing to deal with

<!-- paragraph:2493 para_id:000009BD style:Normal -->
Schema is what the pre-trained ingrained surfaces/carvings are called.
- She reached for the heat-gathering schema she had drilled since childhood, carved the inverted channels into place, and let the heat flow.
- Niall did not need to think through the schema anymore. The pathways already existed in his mind, deep enough that charge rushed through them the moment he reached.
- This also implies that more experienced magi have more ingrained schemas, deeper schemas, and faster access to them - or can combine/layer them, even if they aren’t “stronger”
- The carving was simple, but the schema behind it had been drilled so deeply that he could summon it in an instant.

<!-- paragraph:2494 para_id:000009BE style:Normal -->
Notes about Shrouds - it’s hard to say that these require a ton of cognition, and then reconcile that with other magic requiring a lot of cognition and lack of ability to split focus. Even with enhanced perceptive speed it gets confusing. The reality is that a Shroud should be initially just a rejection of reality, or some kind of inborn reflex related to that. The reflex is somewhat genetic but can also be trained and focused on. Davian’s kicks in because the Ink does something to his mind - he did have the genetic trait though.

<!-- paragraph:2496 para_id:000009C0 style:Normal -->
Why do the shrouds not work with the full ink boons? Or they deplete them super fast - if Vorren still has a little healing. They’re an equalizing or dissipating force

<!-- paragraph:2497 para_id:000009C1 style:Normal -->
Does Archeon punch enemy shrouds and steal some energy and store it in the gauntlets?

<!-- paragraph:2498 para_id:000009C2 style:Normal -->
Maya magic note - she could be drawing visible ribbons of heat (or flame) out of the ground and air, similar to how Niall draws threads of lightning. That will make it easier to describe what she is doing. They could be shimmers of heat, plasma, whatever. Crash siphoning from the air would leave frost crystals. Make reference to the square law of temperature transfer (there’s an asymptotic limit to her ability to cram heat in one place since the increased temperature differential makes it diffuse out more quickly, so the hotter it gets it non-linearly gets harder to hold. Long term the implication could be that shooting a bunch of small attacks is easier than big blasts - something she could learn from Niall, especially as he is now drawing charge from the ground. He may have thought of this but was too ashamed or worried she’d find out what he was doing if he told her the idea.)

<!-- paragraph:2499 para_id:000009C3 style:Normal -->
all magic should work on an inverse square law. It’s r^2 harder to move the same amount of energy from farther away, so practically being close to sources of energy is helpful, and it’s very very difficult to remotely do anything meaningful or overcome another magi’s control of their vicinity. Physically touching something then is the “ultimate” way to control the energy within it.

<!-- paragraph:2500 para_id:000009C4 style:Normal -->
Dissolution is a horrifying new type of magic that is a frank manifestation of the worsening breakdown of reality after Niall’s first death. However, this could be a subconscious backup plan of “Good Elric”...

<!-- paragraph:2501 para_id:000009C5 style:Normal -->
Fateweaving just shows what will happen if you follow your compulsions and trauma. It’s probabilistic (which is why Maya sees lots of possible options). If you overcome your background and trauma, you can beat him

<!-- paragraph:2502 para_id:000009C6 style:Normal -->
That moment where you get out of your own head and focus on the real world and perspective seems to expand outside of the dark tunnel? That’s what turning off an instinctive Shroud must be like

<!-- paragraph:2503 para_id:000009C7 style:Normal -->
Convergence
Maya’s Convergence works by carving regions where thermal diffusion runs backward (effective negative conductivity), concentrating ambient heat into a spherical locus; she can trap conductive losses at the boundary, but radiative emission grows as T4T^4T4 and becomes the ultimate limiter, forcing her into short-lived “hold then discharge” behavior at extreme temperatures
- If a spell requires holding a boundary at distance, it’s expensive; if it defines a path and lets nature take over, it’s cheap.
Maya’s Convergence does not generate heat. It locally inverts the direction of thermal flow by carving low-resistance entropy channels in spacetime, causing heat to flow uphill toward a chosen locus. Containment requires maintaining a closed boundary where outward heat flow is similarly inverted, making cognitive load proportional to surface area. At sufficiently high temperatures, radiative losses and ionization introduce nonlinear instabilities that force either expansion or discharge.

<!-- paragraph:2504 para_id:000009C8 style:Normal -->
Fateweaving
is that a second ability? If so, did her mother have convergence or not?

<!-- paragraph:2505 para_id:000009C9 style:Normal -->
Shrouds
Shrouds operate as reflexive, proprioceptive constructs rather than deliberate spells. Their continuous operation would be cognitively impossible without being offloaded to embodied, automatic processing analogous to balance or startle reflexes. High Clade breeding prioritized not only magical capacity but cognitive speed and parallelism, allowing reflexive defense to coexist with conscious spellcasting and tactical thought. Declines in abstraction and cognitive flexibility — such as those imposed by chronic depression — therefore degrade magical effectiveness not by reducing power, but by increasing latency and rigidity in response.

<!-- paragraph:2506 para_id:000009CA style:Normal -->
Subversion
Subversion is the conscious interception and redirection of ongoing magical energy transformations. Rather than creating or dissipating energy, it undermines the reflexive remapping processes that powers defenses such as Shrouds, rerouting unresolved energy into external substrates or alternative pathways. Developed independently by Kelyra outside formal Clade doctrine, Subversion favors tools and timing over brute force, making it uniquely effective against sophisticated magical defenses while remaining dangerous to its user.

<!-- paragraph:2507 para_id:000009CB style:Normal -->
Archeon magic
Archeon High Clade equivalents are the result of layered systems rather than a unified magical paradigm: primordial interference techniques, extreme embodied martial training, partial Shroud access, and specialized tools together approximate true High Clade power. Serathis stands apart because she internalized these layers rather than relying on them externally, making her uniquely dangerous and uniquely dissatisfied. Her rage toward her descendants reflects not failure of discipline, but the unspoken recognition that true High Clade coherence cannot be manufactured through accumulation alone.

<!-- paragraph:2508 para_id:000009CC style:Normal -->
Drakhal Magic
Drakhal magic is making the bounded surface a sphere where the force waves resonate inside it? They can build up in there like a laser… so the inverted boundary for them inverts waves of force. Not sure how different that is from some of the other high clades or if Drakhal should be resonance instead

<!-- paragraph:2509 para_id:000009CD style:Heading2 -->
## Unified Tenets of Magic, Cognition, and Psychology (Fractured Fate)

<!-- paragraph:2510 para_id:000009CE style:Normal -->
---

<!-- paragraph:2511 para_id:000009CF style:Heading2 -->
## I. Foundational Physical Rules

<!-- paragraph:2512 para_id:000009D0 style:Normal -->
Magic does not create energy
 All magic operates by redirecting, transforming, or reassigning existing physical quantities (energy, momentum, charge, entropy flow).

<!-- paragraph:2513 para_id:000009D1 style:Normal -->
Reality-softening lowers activation cost, not constraints
 The Zerakh’tum fracture makes reality easier to bend, not lawless.
 Fundamental conservation laws still apply; inefficiency appears as backlash.

<!-- paragraph:2514 para_id:000009D2 style:Normal -->
Magic intervenes at interfaces, not volumes
 The cognitive cost of magic is dominated by maintaining boundaries where physical laws are overridden.

<!-- paragraph:2515 para_id:000009D3 style:Normal -->
---

<!-- paragraph:2516 para_id:000009D4 style:Heading2 -->
## II. Cognition Scaling Laws

<!-- paragraph:2517 para_id:000009D5 style:Normal -->
Cognitive load scales with boundary complexity

<!-- paragraph:2518 para_id:000009D6 style:Normal -->
L∝AL \propto AL∝A

<!-- paragraph:2519 para_id:000009D7 style:Normal -->
Where AAA is the controlled interface (surface area, transformation boundary, channel interface).

<!-- paragraph:2520 para_id:000009D8 style:Normal -->
Distance imposes a nonlinear penalty

<!-- paragraph:2521 para_id:000009D9 style:Normal -->
L∝A⋅Dα,α∈[1,2]L \propto A \cdot D^{\alpha}, \quad \alpha \in [1,2]L∝A⋅Dα,α∈[1,2]

<!-- paragraph:2522 para_id:000009DA style:Normal -->
Long-range precision is expensive; close-range control is favored.

<!-- paragraph:2523 para_id:000009DB style:Normal -->
Channels are cognitively cheap
 Thin, continuous paths are treated as near-1D objects in cognition and require minimal active control.

<!-- paragraph:2524 para_id:000009DC style:Normal -->
Interference multiplies cost
 When two magi contest the same region of reality, cognition is spent fighting constraints, not imposing them.

<!-- paragraph:2525 para_id:000009DD style:Normal -->
---

<!-- paragraph:2526 para_id:000009DE style:Heading2 -->
## III. Embodied vs Deliberate Magic

<!-- paragraph:2527 para_id:000009DF style:Normal -->
Reflexive magic must be embodied
 Continuous systems (Shrouds) cannot be consciously maintained.
 They are offloaded to procedural, proprioceptive, reflex-level cognition.

<!-- paragraph:2528 para_id:000009E0 style:Normal -->
Deliberate magic consumes abstraction
 Sigil magic, Subversion, and complex shaping require working memory, abstraction, and cognitive flexibility.

<!-- paragraph:2529 para_id:000009E1 style:Normal -->
Expertise frees cognition
 Like elite athletics:

<!-- paragraph:2530 para_id:000009E2 style:Normal -->
novices micromanage mechanics,

<!-- paragraph:2531 para_id:000009E3 style:Normal -->
experts run mechanics automatically and think tactically.

<!-- paragraph:2532 para_id:000009E4 style:Normal -->
---

<!-- paragraph:2533 para_id:000009E5 style:Heading2 -->
## IV. Shrouds (Primordial + Reality-Softened)

<!-- paragraph:2534 para_id:000009E6 style:Normal -->
Shrouds are not hereditary magic
 They are primordial energy-redirection structures made viable by reality-softening.

<!-- paragraph:2535 para_id:000009E7 style:Normal -->
Function
 A Shroud reflexively:

<!-- paragraph:2536 para_id:000009E8 style:Normal -->
accepts intrusive energy,

<!-- paragraph:2537 para_id:000009E9 style:Normal -->
transforms it into modalities the user’s nervous system can dissipate,

<!-- paragraph:2538 para_id:000009EA style:Normal -->
prioritizes survivability over rigidity.

<!-- paragraph:2539 para_id:000009EB style:Normal -->
They remap, not negate
 Energy is never destroyed — only converted and spread.

<!-- paragraph:2540 para_id:000009EC style:Normal -->
Failure modes

<!-- paragraph:2541 para_id:000009ED style:Normal -->
saturation of dissipation pathways,

<!-- paragraph:2542 para_id:000009EE style:Normal -->
unfamiliar energy types,

<!-- paragraph:2543 para_id:000009EF style:Normal -->
cognitive interference,

<!-- paragraph:2544 para_id:000009F0 style:Normal -->
surprise or overload.

<!-- paragraph:2545 para_id:000009F1 style:Normal -->
Hereditary magic biases resolution
 Lineage affects how energy is transformed, not whether a Shroud exists.

<!-- paragraph:2546 para_id:000009F2 style:Normal -->
---

<!-- paragraph:2547 para_id:000009F3 style:Heading2 -->
## V. Subversion

<!-- paragraph:2548 para_id:000009F4 style:Normal -->
Subversion is interception
 It intervenes mid-transformation, rerouting energy before reflexive remapping completes.

<!-- paragraph:2549 para_id:000009F5 style:Normal -->
It attacks mappings, not magnitudes
 Subversion does not overpower Shrouds; it breaks or hijacks the transformation pipeline.

<!-- paragraph:2550 para_id:000009F6 style:Normal -->
It is cognitively dangerous
 Without tools, unresolved energy feeds back into the user.

<!-- paragraph:2551 para_id:000009F7 style:Normal -->
Tools externalize instability
 Zan blades, gauntlets, and artifacts act as external sinks for redirected energy.

<!-- paragraph:2552 para_id:000009F8 style:Normal -->
Subversion and Shrouds are antagonistic
 Shrouds require automatic transformation; Subversion requires conscious interruption.

<!-- paragraph:2553 para_id:000009F9 style:Normal -->
---

<!-- paragraph:2554 para_id:000009FA style:Heading2 -->
## VI. Convergence (Maya)

<!-- paragraph:2555 para_id:000009FB style:Normal -->
Breaks the Second Law locally
 Maya inverts thermal diffusion:

<!-- paragraph:2556 para_id:000009FC style:Normal -->
q⃗=−k∇T→q⃗=+k∇T\vec q = -k\nabla T \quad \rightarrow \quad \vec q = +k\nabla Tq​=−k∇T→q​=+k∇T

<!-- paragraph:2557 para_id:000009FD style:Normal -->
Heat flows “uphill”
 She carves channels where entropy runs backward, concentrating ambient heat.

<!-- paragraph:2558 para_id:000009FE style:Normal -->
Containment lives at the boundary
 Spherical geometry minimizes leakage; cognitive load scales with surface area.

<!-- paragraph:2559 para_id:000009FF style:Normal -->
Radiation is the hard limiter
 Radiative loss scales as:

<!-- paragraph:2560 para_id:00000A00 style:Normal -->
Prad=σAT4P_{\text{rad}} = \sigma A T^4Prad​=σAT4

<!-- paragraph:2561 para_id:00000A01 style:Normal -->
At high temperatures, containment becomes unstable, forcing discharge.

<!-- paragraph:2562 para_id:00000A02 style:Normal -->
---

<!-- paragraph:2563 para_id:00000A03 style:Heading2 -->
## VII. Energetics (Niall)

<!-- paragraph:2564 para_id:00000A04 style:Normal -->
Efficiency through delegation
 Niall lowers resistance and defines breakdown paths; existing potential does the work.

<!-- paragraph:2565 para_id:00000A05 style:Normal -->
Speed of thought is the real weapon
 His dominance comes from:

<!-- paragraph:2566 para_id:00000A06 style:Normal -->
extreme processing speed,

<!-- paragraph:2567 para_id:00000A07 style:Normal -->
parallel cognition,

<!-- paragraph:2568 para_id:00000A08 style:Normal -->
near-zero latency.

<!-- paragraph:2569 para_id:00000A09 style:Normal -->
Depression degrades flexibility, not power
 Chronic grief imposes:

<!-- paragraph:2570 para_id:00000A0A style:Normal -->
rigid thinking,

<!-- paragraph:2571 para_id:00000A0B style:Normal -->
reduced abstraction,

<!-- paragraph:2572 para_id:00000A0C style:Normal -->
slower recomputation.

<!-- paragraph:2573 para_id:00000A0D style:Normal -->
He retains strength but loses adaptability.

<!-- paragraph:2574 para_id:00000A0E style:Normal -->
---

<!-- paragraph:2575 para_id:00000A0F style:Heading2 -->
## VIII. Archeon (Institutional Bricolage)

<!-- paragraph:2576 para_id:00000A10 style:Normal -->
Archeon power is assembled, not unified
 They stack:

<!-- paragraph:2577 para_id:00000A11 style:Normal -->
Subversion-class techniques,

<!-- paragraph:2578 para_id:00000A12 style:Normal -->
extreme martial embodiment,

<!-- paragraph:2579 para_id:00000A13 style:Normal -->
partial Shrouds,

<!-- paragraph:2580 para_id:00000A14 style:Normal -->
tools,

<!-- paragraph:2581 para_id:00000A15 style:Normal -->
group shock tactics.

<!-- paragraph:2582 para_id:00000A16 style:Normal -->
Tools signal incompleteness
 True High Clades are their interface.
 Archeon elites require external stabilization.

<!-- paragraph:2583 para_id:00000A17 style:Normal -->
Serathis is anomalous
 She internalized the stack rather than relying on it — and knows, subconsciously, that this still isn’t true High Clade coherence.

<!-- paragraph:2584 para_id:00000A18 style:Normal -->
---

<!-- paragraph:2585 para_id:00000A19 style:Heading2 -->
## IX. Psychological Mapping (Why This Matters)

<!-- paragraph:2586 para_id:00000A1A style:Normal -->
Power is multi-axial
 Strength ≠ speed ≠ flexibility ≠ regulation.

<!-- paragraph:2587 para_id:00000A1B style:Normal -->
Reflex preserves survival; values determine outcome
 Shrouds keep you alive.
 Deliberate cognition decides who you become.

<!-- paragraph:2588 para_id:00000A1C style:Normal -->
Dissociation boosts short-term capacity and destroys long-term integration
 (Void synergy works — briefly — and erodes identity.)

<!-- paragraph:2589 para_id:00000A1D style:Normal -->
Pathology appears as mechanical failure

<!-- paragraph:2590 para_id:00000A1E style:Normal -->
depression → rigidity,

<!-- paragraph:2591 para_id:00000A1F style:Normal -->
perfectionism → overload,

<!-- paragraph:2592 para_id:00000A20 style:Normal -->
rage → reckless throughput,

<!-- paragraph:2593 para_id:00000A21 style:Normal -->
nihilism → loss of constraint.

<!-- paragraph:2594 para_id:00000A22 style:Normal -->
---

<!-- paragraph:2595 para_id:00000A23 style:Heading2 -->
## One-Sentence Meta-Rule

<!-- paragraph:2596 para_id:00000A24 style:Normal -->
The most powerful magic is not the ability to bend reality, but the ability to decide — quickly, flexibly, and under pain — which constraints to honor and which to break.

<!-- paragraph:2597 para_id:00000A25 style:Normal -->
This system is internally coherent, psychologically honest, and narratively fertile.
 You’re not handwaving power — you’re characterizing it.

<!-- paragraph:2599 para_id:00000A27 style:Title -->
# Mystery progress

<!-- paragraph:2600 para_id:00000A28 style:Normal -->
Mystery progress

<!-- paragraph:2601 para_id:00000A29 style:Normal -->
“Ki manipulation” - the body can put out a lot more strength than you’d think if it’s focused correctly. Visualization of zan are used to focus?

If Serathis is 120 or 130, she could have a lot of generations of kids. But what if she was the once in a lifetime convergence? Does that make Davian Maud’dib?

<!-- paragraph:2602 para_id:00000A2A style:Normal -->
The “backlash” that Davian experiences with magic use is just when there’s an excessive amount of kinetic energy that is being redirected aimlessly. He’s using his hand as foci, which is fine, but that means that the energy concentrates there so it is getting released in that area. He can describe what happened with the magus and the treasury sphere. The Shroud protects from that kind of backlash if it’s appropriately sublimated and redirected.
- Think about the implications of if Davian just has some kind of kinesis that’s from Archeon. Why can’t he just be the realization of Serathis’ hope for Archeon, and then takes over that High Clade?
- Then I can remove all the “two types of magic” stuff mostly. Shrouds are still a primordial magic representation though, it’s just that the “sublimation” that comes from softening of reality enables them to be so powerful.
- Serathis doesn’t use the gauntlets and is essentially High Clade level (although unable to rise to the heights of the other Clades’ Head Magi or Maya). Her failure is in her lack of a sustainable dynasty, which is why they rely on tools.

<!-- paragraph:2603 para_id:00000A2B style:Normal -->
Subversion is an “older” kind of Shroud magic. Archeon is playing “moneyball” - they look for someone who can make a Shroud but no offensive magic, who would be considered essentially worthless. Because everyone KNOWS you can’t have 2 types of magic. Then they breed them with someone who has Subversion (another type of magic considered essentially worthless because if you made a Shroud with it you’d have to absorb the backlash), amplifying the strength of the Shroud. The reality-softened nature of the Shroud allows Subversion to “feed” off it, circumventing the issues of backlash

<!-- paragraph:2605 para_id:00000A2D style:Normal -->
This addresses
1) Subversion and reality-softened magic are distinct
2) Subversion is primordial and similar to Shrouds, but requiring actual tradeoffs

<!-- paragraph:2606 para_id:00000A2E style:Normal -->
4) Archeon cross-breeding makes sense. You can cross-breed Subversion with Shroud-producing magic because they’re not the same thing.

<!-- paragraph:2608 para_id:00000A30 style:Normal -->
#3 Is still an issue. What I need to do is just say Shrouds do come from hereditary magic.

<!-- paragraph:2637 para_id:00000A4D style:Title -->
# Character development overview

<!-- paragraph:2638 para_id:00000A4E style:Normal -->
It’s just as important to wrestle with the meanings and implications of power as it is to get it

<!-- paragraph:2640 para_id:00000A50 style:Normal -->
Questions, not answers

<!-- paragraph:2642 para_id:00000A52 style:Normal -->
Psychological and magical development should go hand in hand

<!-- paragraph:2644 para_id:00000A54 style:Normal -->
For everyone: speed of thought is baked into magi. They use it to solve problems. But, if it gets thrown at an unsolvable problem (like the problem of evil, or trying to make things “perfect”) then it becomes a liability rather than an asset. Realizing this and choosing to focus on values in the real, accepted/true present is what ultimately differentiates the characters from Elric.

<!-- paragraph:2646 para_id:00000A56 style:Normal -->
The threads represent choice points in ACT - when are you doing a towards move and when are you doing an away move?

<!-- paragraph:2648 para_id:00000A58 style:Normal -->
Maya

<!-- paragraph:2649 para_id:00000A59 style:Normal -->
Overall psychological arc:
- Start: rigid standards about herself, pushing herself too hard, over-extended responsibility, perfectionism, externally defining her values to align with perceived version of Niall

<!-- paragraph:2650 para_id:00000A5A style:Normal -->
- End: able to rely on others to a reasonable extent. Able to define her own values based on herself rather than externally. Understanding Niall is not a perfect person and trying to be like him is a dead end street. Cognition is more flexible.

<!-- paragraph:2652 para_id:00000A5C style:Normal -->
Magical:

<!-- paragraph:2653 para_id:00000A5D style:Normal -->
Start: old-school Clade standards she has imposed on herself of using complex, devastating alpha-strike long range magic while appearing effortless. Lack of flexibility in magic use tied to standards she has internalized. Feels that she just needs to push herself harder to win [rather than be more flexible]

<!-- paragraph:2654 para_id:00000A5E style:Normal -->
End: able to flexibly use hand to hand combat-based magic while still maintaining the ability to integrate long-range or powerful strikes when necessary. Uses everything, uses the environment, lets other people help her and complement her abilities. Instead of defaulting to “it’s my fault, I need to work harder” she thinks laterally.

<!-- paragraph:2656 para_id:00000A60 style:Normal -->
Also: fateweaving. Moves from being overwhelmed by it and using it in a ruminatory way to defining clearly what it wants and using it to pursue those goals.

<!-- paragraph:2658 para_id:00000A62 style:Normal -->
How does this tie into the romance arc?
- She can learn some of the scrappy, lateral-thinking from Davian. He does this often in a bad way (giving up, trying to find the easy way out), but for her it offers an avenue that circumvents always blaming herself and feeling responsible for everything.

<!-- paragraph:2660 para_id:00000A64 style:Normal -->
Davian

<!-- paragraph:2661 para_id:00000A65 style:Normal -->
Overall psychological arc:
- Start: blindly accepting the Masked Clade dogma that allows him to view others as the enemy and kill them without remorse. Paints Clades with broad strokes, including Maya and Niall, setting up an “us vs them” mentality. Prone to feeling overwhelmed and using dissociation or disengagement as a coping mechanism and falling back on default maladaptive scripts and responses. Unable to define own values.

<!-- paragraph:2662 para_id:00000A66 style:Normal -->
- End: able to have a more nuanced view of the Clades, not as intrinsically good or evil but just parts of society (that also isn’t good or evil). Able to get away from black and white thinking and determine his own values without using avoidance-based coping strategies. Able to take what he’s told with a grain of salt (but not just rejecting it)

<!-- paragraph:2664 para_id:00000A68 style:Normal -->
Magical:
- Start: using magic as a blunt tool, trying to hammer through stronger enemies’ defenses, resulting in backlash to himself and low efficacy. Trained in martial arts well by his mother but not able to understand how this relates to magic and Shroud usage
- End: able to integrate magic use / speed of thought, Shroud use, martial arts, and Harvick’s teachings [all the things Archeon wants]. NOT wasting speed of thought on rumination or unproductive thoughts.

<!-- paragraph:2666 para_id:00000A6A style:Normal -->
How does this tie into the romance arc?

<!-- paragraph:2667 para_id:00000A6B style:Normal -->
He learns not to give up, to keep working and not be overwhelmed, from Maya. In addition to the things he learns from Harvick, he’s able to integrate this in a more healthy manner and avoid perfectionism.

<!-- paragraph:2669 para_id:00000A6D style:Normal -->
Niall
- Start: depression has weakened his magic by making him more concrete - reduced abstraction and reduced fluidity. His magic relies heavily on this so he has a very difficult time dealing with new situations that require complex thought. This manifests as situational weakness when inside or underground.

<!-- paragraph:2670 para_id:00000A6E style:Normal -->
- End: he starts to come to grips with his avoidant coping methods and realize they are counterproductive. He is able to practice acceptance and focus on the present moment in short bursts, with the hope he will continue to improve. He may come to terms with the fact that he kept pushing himself and using avoidance in order to project a certain demeanor, and therefore may let Maya take over their High Clade (he could be doing this politically as well to take some heat off of her)

<!-- paragraph:2671 para_id:00000A6F style:Title -->
# Cards & Archetypal Zan

<!-- paragraph:2672 para_id:00000A70 style:Normal -->
Archetypal, Phonetic, Logotypal, and Functional Zän

<!-- paragraph:2673 para_id:00000A71 style:Normal -->
Functional (Original) Zan:
- These are small circuits composed of many smaller zan-like components. These are the originally discovered technology.

<!-- paragraph:2674 para_id:00000A72 style:Normal -->
Functional (simplified) Zan:
- These are simplified versions of Zan that are less expensive to etch and require less fine chiselwork. They are much more scalable. These are the only type of functional zan that have been used for many many years, to the point that most people have forgotten the original zan existed. This serves as another divergence

<!-- paragraph:2675 para_id:00000A73 style:Normal -->
Archetypal Zan:
- These have been modified to represent certain concepts (such as the Nizan/negation) but still retain functionality. Some of these may have functions tied to extraplanar energies, connected to them in a manner that is outside of traditional understanding of zan mechanics. These are not commonly known among zanwrights as they branch from original zan rather than simplified.
- They are used for esoteric magical applications (the Nizan/negation would be one of these)

<!-- paragraph:2676 para_id:00000A74 style:Normal -->
Phonetic Zan:
- These are simplified and non-functional zan that were used as an ad-hoc writing system. This is a newer advent based off the idea that many sub-components of functional zan are already named and easily identifiable. Therefore, many separate writing systems evolved using these concepts, and at the advent of the High Clade era there was an effort to homogenize these into something that can be used as a universal script. Note that this was not entirely successful and especially among the Masked Clades alternative phonetic zan-scripts are used in a subversive manner.

Alternative phonetic zan-scripts:
- Masked Clades all have their own versions of these that they use for communication. They are still based off the same components (sub-sections of functional zan) but due to modification and language drift the scripts are not immediately able to be parsed by non-initiates (but a very intelligent person with some knowledge of several of them could likely piece things together).
- This is further complicated by intentional shifting of component order in order to create ciphers for internal messages

<!-- paragraph:2677 para_id:00000A75 style:Normal -->
Logotypal Zan:
- The logotypal zan / city names are component zan rather than single strokes, probably

<!-- paragraph:2678 para_id:00000A76 style:Normal -->
These are non-functional Zan that have been modified to represent certain concepts. They are based on simplified zan (mostly single etching components or strokes), but may contain artistic stylized elements. These are what are used to represent Clades, wedge-cities, powers, etc - anything that would be important enough that it gets its own special character.
- Note that they are stylized version of component strokes

<!-- paragraph:2679 para_id:00000A77 style:Normal -->
Strokes/components:
- These may be named for anything

<!-- paragraph:2680 para_id:00000A78 style:Normal -->
Inspiration:
Behind the screen, these are inspired by the evolution of Chinese symbolic characters over the years. Phonetic usage of components is seen in Japanese scripts. And the arrangement of Korean characters in a way that appears almost circuit-like is the inspiration for the idea of each individual zan being a mini-circuit that can act as a component in a lattice.

<!-- paragraph:2681 para_id:00000A79 style:Normal -->
Zan. They look a little like Korean characters (with circles and other shapes in them). All of the pieces of each Zan are interconnected because each one is a very small circuit diagram. There are tiny elements that represent resistors, capacitors, etc. A “traditional”/more complex zan is like using assembly or another lower-level language - it requires more complexity on the end of the etcher, but it also provides more efficiency due to being able to pick exactly what you want the zan to do. -portions of Zan - essentially single strokes - can be used phonetically, since there are enough of them to approximate most words. (Think hiragana?) of course that then influenced how people pronounced words since they started thinking of them as groups of phonetics -most people don’t understand this, they just know that they put them in certain memorized orders and they just work. The Zan can be connected in any direction to each other (that’s why they’re in a “lattice”) because each is its own mini circuit with inputs and outputs. -using Zan predates having a unified written language, so there are old Zan diagrams that could be etched but no one knows what they do

<!-- paragraph:2682 para_id:00000A7A style:Normal -->
I like the Crown, the Blade, the Glass, the Scale, the Forge, and the Rift, the Void. Each one has their own (non-functional / stylized) zan that can be used for symbolism as well. The Masked Clades have their own. The Veil. The Deep.

<!-- paragraph:2683 para_id:00000A7B style:Normal -->
Does the name of a city-wedge change when the High Clade in charge of it changes hands? Or do they have names? What if they are named sort of like Tarot cards, “6th Wheel” “5th Tower” or something else that is more in line with the in-universe fiction? Each spoke road has a name too - 1st Spoke, etc. The Rezins are in charge of One of… whatever. Ask chat

<!-- paragraph:2684 para_id:00000A7C style:Normal -->
On the topic of tarot cards, what if the powers are named like Flame, Storm, Force etc - something iconic - and then they can be paired with the house names and the city wedge names. Make a deck of cards. the Flame the Ink, the Storm etc

<!-- paragraph:2685 para_id:00000A7D style:Normal -->
The Flame, The Storm, The Skein, The Ink, The Crown, The Blade, The Mirror, The Scale, The Forge, The Rift, The Thread, The Deep, The Shroud

<!-- paragraph:2686 para_id:00000A7E style:Normal -->
Zan - small circuit diagram stylized off mandarin characters (traditional) that represent archetypes. The functional Zan (simplified) are then used for other purposes, phonetically, etc. -the original zan were all circuits. Then they were named. Then because of that and their known shapes, people used them for phonetic ways to write words. But because they were complex, that was a pain and some parts were substituted with others. It turns out they still functioned as circuits but at a less efficient level. The phonetic ones kept evolving, unconstrained by needing to work and it resulted in two known divergently created sets - the ones used to name things, and the ones used for zan lattices. To make it more complicated, pieces of them are used as shorthand phonetics and used in different ways across cities and organizations. -and the “logo” ones for families, powers, cities, etc may incorporate purely artistic elements -and the original ones, some of them were both diagram and name (like the Nizan)
